NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
My daughter, J. Deepalakshmi a Female child born to Th. B. Jayakumar & Tmt. J. Usha on 17th November 2004,
Residing at Old No. 5, New No. 10, Duraisamy Street, Vetry Nagar, Chennai-600 082 has been living as a male after natural
evolution of testicles representing of a male gender. Detailed analysis be a panel of Senior Civil Surgeon of Rajiv Gandhi
Government General Hospital, Chennai-600 003, Reveals that due to Chromosom Changes, her gender has changed to that
of a male. By this he may be treated as a male and shall henceforth be known as J. DEEPAK KUMAR.
Chennai,
J. USHA.
29th April 2016.
 (Mother.)
